---

## Part 3: Quality Pass Standard

These criteria define pass/fail for each bible study entry after re-migration.

### 1. Content Exists

- **Rule:** If an entry has a Q-type attachment file on disk, the DB `questions` field MUST be non-empty.
- **Rule:** If an entry has an N-type attachment file on disk, the DB `answers` field MUST be non-empty.
- **Rule:** If an entry has an M-type attachment file on disk, the DB `transcript` field MUST be non-empty.
- **Exception:** Entries with no attachments (8 total) are allowed to have empty content fields.
- **Exception:** Entries with missing files (4 total) are allowed to have empty content fields for the missing file type.

### 2. Format

- **Rule:** All content fields (`questions`, `answers`, `transcript`) MUST contain valid TipTap JSON.
- **Check:** Content must start with `{"type":"doc"` and be parseable as JSON.
- **Fail:** Raw HTML tags visible as text (e.g., `<p>`, `<b>`, `<br>`).
- **Fail:** Content stored as plain HTML string (not wrapped in TipTap JSON structure).

### 3. Font Preservation

- **Rule:** If the source document uses serif fonts (Times New Roman, Georgia, etc.), the TipTap JSON must include `textStyle` marks with `fontFamily` attribute.
- **Rule:** If the source document uses sans-serif fonts (Arial, Calibri, etc.), the TipTap JSON should also preserve `fontFamily` where specified.
- **Context:** Most pre-2016 documents use Times New Roman (serif). Post-2016 documents typically use Calibri or Arial (sans-serif). The migration pipeline must detect and preserve the dominant font.
- **Note:** Font detection should examine the source .doc/.docx/.rtf file metadata or content, not guess from date.

### 4. No Garbled Content

- **Rule:** Content must not contain binary data, WPC format artifacts, or encoding errors.
- **Check:** No sequences of non-printable characters, no `\x00` null bytes, no runs of `?` or replacement characters.
- **Known risk:** 3 WPC-format files (`Js5b2003Q.doc`, `Js5a2003N.doc`, `Lk19a2003N.doc`) will produce garbled output if processed as standard .doc.
- **Known risk:** 6 RTF-disguised-as-.doc files need RTF conversion path, not .doc conversion.

### 5. Indent Preservation

- **Rule:** Numbered questions with hanging indents must be preserved in the TipTap JSON.
- **Check:** Questions formatted as numbered lists (e.g., "1. What did Jesus...") must retain their indentation structure.
- **Check:** Sub-questions with deeper indentation must be correctly nested.
- **Implementation:** Use the TipTap Indent extension with `hangingIndent` support.

### 6. RTF Support

- **Rule:** All 80 `.rtf` attachment files must be successfully converted and imported.
- **Rule:** The 6 RTF-disguised-as-.doc files must also be handled via RTF conversion.
- **Total:** 86 files requiring RTF conversion pipeline.
- **Status:** RTF files were NOT imported in the initial migration. This is a gap that must be closed.

### 7. Completeness

- **Rule:** All 1180 entries must have a corresponding `BibleStudy` row in the database.
- **Rule:** All attachment files that exist on disk must have a corresponding `BibleStudyAttachment` record.
- **Rule:** Content from each attachment must be imported into the correct DB field (Q->questions, N->answers, M->transcript).

---

## Part 4: Edge Cases

### 4.1 Files Missing from Disk (4 files)

These attachment references exist in the parsed data but the files are not present in `00_old_laubf_db_dump/files/`.

| legacyId | slug | title | passage | date | Missing File | Impact |
|----------|------|-------|---------|------|--------------|--------|
| 8862 | what-is-impossible-with-man-is-possible-with-god | "What is impossible with man is possible with God." | Luke 18:18-30 | 2020-01-05 | `NewYear-2020(2)Inductive.docx` | Q field will be empty |
| 8914 | jesus-a-horn-of-salvation | Jesus, A horn of Salvation | Luke 1:67-80 | 2020-12-13 | `XmasLK1-2020Q.docx` | Q field will be empty |
| 8918 | the-lord-knows-how-to-rescue-the-godly | The Lord knows how to rescue the godly | 2Peter 2:1-12 | 2021-01-10 | `2Pet2A-2020Q.docx` | Q field will be empty |
| 8944 | rehoboam-and-jeroboam | Rehoboam and Jeroboam | 1Kings 12:1-33 | 2021-06-06 | `1ki12-2021P (3).pptx` | Presentation only, not content |

### 4.2 WordPerfect (WPC) Format Files (3 files)

These files use WordPerfect format disguised with `.doc` extension. Standard conversion tools (mammoth, libreoffice doc mode) will produce garbled binary output.

**Required handling:** Use LibreOffice with explicit WordPerfect import filter, or use a dedicated WPC-to-text converter.

| legacyId | slug | title | passage | date | File |
|----------|------|-------|---------|------|------|
| 8773 | the-fall-of-jericho | The Fall of Jericho | Joshua 5:13-6:27 | 2003-02-09 | `Js5b2003Q.doc` |
| 8774 | circumcision-at-gilgal | Circumcision at Gilgal | Joshua 5:1-12 | 2003-02-02 | `Js5a2003N.doc` |
| 8778 | a-very-small-thing | A Very small thing | Luke 19:11-27 | 2003-01-05 | `Lk19a2003N.doc` |

### 4.3 RTF Files Disguised as .doc (6 files)

These files have `.doc` extension but contain RTF content. The migration pipeline must detect RTF magic bytes (`{\rtf`) and route these through RTF conversion instead of .doc conversion.

| legacyId | slug | title | passage | date | File |
|----------|------|-------|---------|------|------|
| 8482 | the-faith-of-abraham | The Faith of Abraham | Hebrews 11:8-22 | 2008-04-27 | `Heb11e2008M.doc` |
| 8486 | the-faith-of-enoch | The Faith of Enoch | Hebrews 11:5-6 | 2008-04-13 | `Heb11c2008Q.doc` |
| 8488 | the-faith-of-abel | The Faith of Abel | Hebrews 11:4-4 | 2008-04-06 | `Heb11b2008M.doc` |
| 8498 | he-is-able | He Is Able | Hebrews 2:5-18 | 2008-01-20 | `Heb2a2008M.doc` |
| 8704 | the-world-was-not-worthy-of-them-2 | The world was not worthy of them | Hebrews 11:32-40 | 2004-05-16 | `Hb11c2004N.doc` |
| 8736 | such-great-faith | Such Great faith | Luke 7:1-10 | 2003-10-26 | `Lk7a2003Q.doc` |

### 4.4 RTF Files Not Imported (80 files)

All 80 `.rtf` files were skipped during the initial migration. They span 34 entries, mostly from 2003-2008 era. All have been validated as proper RTF format.

See the RTF File Inventory table in Part 2 for the complete list.

Combined with the 6 RTF-as-.doc files, **86 files total** need RTF conversion support.

### 4.5 Entries with Message/Transcript Attachments (624 entries)

These entries have M-type (Message/Transcript) attachment files. The `transcript` field in the DB must be populated from these files.

This is a large number -- 624 out of 1180 entries (53%) have transcripts. Most entries from 2003-2017 have M files; the pattern dropped off after 2017.

### 4.6 Entries with No Attachments (8 entries)

These entries exist in the parsed data but have zero attachment files. They are conference entries or special events where materials were not uploaded as individual documents.

See the "Entries with No Attachments" table in Part 2 for the complete list.

### 4.7 UNKNOWN Type Attachments (213 attachments across 209 entries)

These attachment filenames could not be automatically classified as Q/N/M based on filename suffix patterns. They fall into several categories:

#### Category A: Single-file entries with no type suffix (5 entries, pre-2015)
Files like `Josh2_2019.docx`, `Lk13d-2015.docx`, `2Sa23b_2014.docx` -- these are standalone study documents without Q/N/M differentiation. Import as questions.

#### Category B: QS_ and BSN_ prefix format (10 files, 2022 era)
Files like `QS_Revelation_1_9-20.docx` and `BSN_Revelation_1_9-20.docx`. QS = Question Sheet (treat as Q), BSN = Bible Study Notes (treat as N).

#### Category C: New naming convention without suffix (160+ files, 2022-2026)
Files like `Matthew5_1_6_QS_22.docx`, `Acts5_01-42_QS_22.docx`, `John1_1-5_QS_24.docx`. These use the `_QS_YY` suffix pattern. QS = Question Sheet (treat as Q).

#### Category D: Inductive study format (20+ files, 2020)
Files like `Mk8b-2020Inductive.docx`. These are inductive Bible study questions (treat as Q).

#### Category E: Special naming (misc)
Files like `James_4_Bible_study.docx`, `Mark9cM_THE SERVANT OF ALL_9_2020.docx`, `matthew12-46-50.docx`. Require manual classification or content inspection.

### 4.8 Duplicate Filenames (9 cases)

See the "Duplicate Filenames" table in Part 2. These require deduplication during import to avoid overwriting content.

### 4.9 Uppercase .DOC Extension (2 files)

`Jn17c2003M.DOC` and `Jn10a2003M.DOC` -- file lookups must be case-insensitive or normalize extensions.

#### 9104: My Spirit Shall Not Contend Forever
